\paragraph{Object and quantities proof-documentation workflow.} This section is generated from the object proof-dossier records in the Master YAML. It is the proofbook infrastructure. Every registered object or quantity has an object-owned dossier. Phase scratchpads remain phase-owned implementation records; object lifecycle fields preserve non-destructive patch, rename, deletion and supersession history. A dossier is not automatically a Lean proof; it records the source objects, definition, proof target, proof sketch, lifecycle status and verification status that must be checked against code. Blue objects may be proof-carrying yet semantically/API-unfinished; their dossier must state that gap before any public-final promotion.

\small
\arrayrulecolor{black!22}

Red transition records failed modules/\allowbreak{}log references, blocks merge/\allowbreak{}deploy, updates the attempted phase to R, creates a repair phase before the blocked phase with source dependencies/\allowbreak{}object-link policy/\allowbreak{}scratchpad/\allowbreak{}dossier stubs, and activates it if dependencies are known. Green transition records build/\allowbreak{}scanner/\allowbreak{}artifact evidence, marks the phase G, updates linked object/\allowbreak{}dossier/\allowbreak{}scratchpad rows only through registered evidence fields, computes the first non-green phase whose dependencies are complete, and sets it active while keeping all other non-green phases non-active.\\
\hline\addlinespace[0.20em]
Verification /\allowbreak{} audit & Planned. Requires red and green fixture runs, manifest validation, YAML patch diffs, failure-history snapshot checks, no-current-deploy checks and cursor uniqueness check.\\
\hline\addlinespace[0.20em]
Next documentation action & Define phase\_state\_transition\_manifest.json and red\_failure\_snapshot.json schemas, plus dry-run examples for red and green transitions.\\
